	// Creature Modifiers



	//Avenger: When one dies, those that remain alive gain bonuses to their visual size, damage, and movement/attack speed.
	//	Implementation: OnDeath find units in radius of the same unit name and apply scale and mofifier.
	// TODO: Proper scale with LoadFromKeyValues (as there is no GetModelScale method in Source 2 for some reason)

	"affix_avenger"
	{
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityTextureName"			"affix_avenger"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_PASSIVE"

		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"attack_speed_bonus"	"25"
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"move_speed_bonus"		"25"
			}
		}

		"Modifiers"
		{
			"modifier_avenger"
			{
				"Passive"	"1"
				"IsHidden"	"1"
				"IsBuff"	"1"	

				"OnDeath"
				{
					"RunScript"		
					{	
						"ScriptFile"	"abilities.lua"
						"Function"		"AvengeDeath"
					}
				}
			}

			"modifier_avenge_me"
			{

				}	
			}
		}

	//Extra Health: Extra Health grants a 50% hit point bonus to Champions, as well as Bosses and their minions. This property is dangerous when it extends fights, and players used to killing monsters quickly enough to avoid real trouble from their damaging properties such as Plagued or Arcane Enchanted may need to retreat or take a different tactic when dealing with Extra Health enemies.
	//Implementation: Spawn with a modifier that does SetMaxHealth and SetHealth	

	"affix_extra_health"
	{
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityTextureName"			"affix_extra_health"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_PASSIVE"

		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"health_bonus_percentage"	"50"
			}
		}

		"precache"
		{
			"particle"	"particles/econ/courier/courier_shagbark/courier_shagbark_ambient.vpcf"
		}

		"Modifiers"
		{
			"modifier_extra_health"
			{
				"Passive"	"1"
				"IsHidden"	"1"

				//unnecessary effect, might remove later
				"EffectName"		"particles/econ/courier/courier_shagbark/courier_shagbark_ambient.vpcf"
				"EffectAttachType"	"follow_origin"
				"OnCreated"
				{
					"RunScript"		
					{	
						"ScriptFile"	"abilities.lua"
						"Function"		"ExtraHealth"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	// Knockback: This modifier grants the boss or champion a knockback attack which will send a character, pet or follower flying away from the monster that hits them. 
	//This is not a slight stumbling bump backwards, as many normal monsters can land; it's a special hit and knocks the target back a considerable distance, often half the screen or further.
	// The real danger comes in the debuff, since knocked back characters and pets are confused, slowing their movement speed for a second after the impact. 
	// Characters can be knocked back into other dangerous effects such as Molten or Arcane and die while still badly slowed.
	// Implementation: Knockback

	"affix_knockback"
	{
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityTextureName"			"affix_knockback"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_PASSIVE"

		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"chance"				"10"
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"slow_duration"			"5"
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"slow_percentage"		"-50"
			}
		}

		"precache"
		{
			"particle"	"particles/status_fx/status_effect_legion_commander_duel.vpcf"
			"particle"	"particles/units/heroes/hero_wisp/wisp_tether_slow.vpcf"
		}
		
		"Modifiers"	
		{
			"modifier_knockback"
			{
				"IsHidden"	"1"
				"Passive"	"1"
				"StatusEffectName"	"particles/status_fx/status_effect_legion_commander_duel.vpcf"
				"StatusEffectPriority"	"1"

				"OnAttackLanded"
				{
					"Random"
					{
						"Chance"	"%chance"
						"OnSuccess"
						{
							"Knockback"
							{
								"Target"	"TARGET"
								"Duration"	"0.5"
								"Distance"	"250"
								"IsFixedDistance" "0"
								"Height"	"50"
				        		"ShouldStun" "0"
							}
							"ApplyModifier"
							{
								"ModifierName"	"modifier_knockback_slow"
								"Target"	"TARGET"
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}

			"modifier_knockback_slow"
			{
				"IsDebuff"		"1"
				"Duration"		"%slow_duration"
				"EffectName"	"particles/units/heroes/hero_wisp/wisp_tether_slow.vpcf"
				"EffectAttachType"	"follow_origin"
				"Properties"
				{
					"MODIFIER_PROPERTY_MOVESPEED_BONUS_PERCENTAGE" "%slow_percentage"
				}
			}
		}
	}

	// Nightmarish: When Nightmarish bosses hit a target with a melee or ranged attack, they have a chance to inflict Fear, Characters or minions so affected will run for a second in a straight line 
	//(if possible) directly away from the champion, boss, or boss' minion that caused the effect.  While running, players have no control over their character.
	// If the running direction is blocked by a wall or other monsters, characters may simply stand still, a complete sitting duck to all enemy attacks.
	// Implementation: Passive OnAttackLanded apply TBR Warlord disorient with a common restricted
	"affix_nightmarish"
	{
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityTextureName"			"affix_nightmarish"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_PASSIVE"

		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"chance"				"10"
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"fear_duration"			"4"
			}
		}

		"precache"
		{
			"particle"	"particles/units/heroes/hero_night_stalker/nightstalker_crippling_fear.vpcf"
			"particle"	"particles/warchasers/nightmarish/axe_battle_hunger.vpcf"
			"particle"	"particles/status_fx/status_effect_fiendsgrip.vpcf"
		}
		
		"Modifiers"	
		{
			"modifier_nightmarish"
			{
				"IsHidden"	"1"
				"Passive"	"1"
				"StatusEffectName"	"particles/units/heroes/hero_night_stalker/nightstalker_crippling_fear.vpcf"
				"StatusEffectPriority"	"1"

				"OnAttackLanded"
				{
					"Random"
					{
						"Chance"	"%chance"
						"OnSuccess"
						{
							"RunScript"
							{
								"ScriptFile"	"abilities.lua"
								"Function"		"Disorient"
							}
							"ApplyModifier"
							{
								"ModifierName"	"modifier_disoriented"
								"Target"	"TARGET"
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}

			"modifier_disoriented"
			{
				"IsDebuff"		"1"
				"Duration"		"%fear_duration"
				"StatusEffectName"	"particles/status_fx/status_effect_fiendsgrip.vpcf"
				"StatusEffectPriority"	"10"

				"EffectName"		"particles/warchasers/nightmarish/axe_battle_hunger.vpcf"
				"EffectAttachType"	"follow_overhead"
				"States"
				{
					"MODIFIER_STATE_COMMAND_RESTRICTED" "MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
				}
				"ThinkInterval"		"2"
				"OnIntervalThink"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"abilities.lua"
						"Function"		"Disorient"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	// Reflects Damage: Reflects Damage, is a higher level boss and champion modifier that causes players to take some damage for every point of damage they deal to enemies. Unlike Thorns, this damage hurts ranged attackers and even spell users.
	// Implementation: OnTakeDamage RunScript with a percentage
	"affix_reflect_damage"
	{
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityTextureName"			"affix_reflect_damage"
		"AbilityUnitDamageType"			"DAMAGE_TYPE_PURE"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_PASSIVE"

		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"damage_percent"		"10"
			}
		}

		"precache"
		{
			"particle"	"particles/items_fx/blademail.vpcf"
		}
		
		"Modifiers"	
		{
			"modifier_reflect_damage"
			{
				"Passive"			"1"
				"EffectName"		"particles/items_fx/blademail.vpcf"
				"EffectAttachType"	"follow_origin"
				"OnTakeDamage"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"DamageAmount"		"%attack_damage"
						"ReflectAmount"		"%damage_percent"
						"ScriptFile"		"abilities.lua"
						"Function"			"ReflectDamage"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	// Vampiric: Vampiric is a sort of monster life leech, enabling them to heal as they deal damage. The amount of healing is fairly minor, making this one of the less-difficult or noticeable boss modifiers. In practice it just makes the enemy feel as though they have slightly higher than normal hit points, and gives some utility to stun or freeze effects, since monsters not dealing damage will not heal Vampire style.
	// Implementation: OnAttackLanded Lifesteal
	"affix_vampiric"
	{
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityTextureName"			"affix_vampiric"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_PASSIVE"

		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"lifesteal"				"30"
			}
		}

		"precache"

			"particle"	"particles/units/heroes/hero_life_stealer/life_stealer_feast.vpcf"
		}
		
		"Modifiers"	
		{
			"modifier_vampiric"
			{
				"IsHidden"	"1"
				"Passive"	"1"

				"OnAttackLanded"
				{
					"Lifesteal"
					{	
						"Target" 				"ATTACKER"
						"LifestealPercent"		"%lifesteal"
					}
					"FireEffect"
					{
						"EffectName"			"particles/units/heroes/hero_life_stealer/life_stealer_feast.vpcf"
						"EffectAttachType"		"attach_hitloc"
						"Target"				"TARGET"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	// Active Modifiers

	//Desecrator: Desecrators create an orange-colored "glowing void zone" beneath the feet of a character. These function like small Firewalls, dealing damage to any character who stands in them.
	//The void zones take a second or so to come into effect, giving a visual warning so players have time to move, assuming they are not blocked in by modifiers like Waller or Jailer.
	//The Desecrated pools remain in place for 12 seconds, and during battles with minions all casting Desecration, entire screens can be come virtually impassable due to the pits of damage.
	//Implementation: CreateThinker with jakiro lava that does damage OnIntervalThink
	// TODO: AI

	"affix_desecrator"

	// Frozen: Frozen spawns on Champions, Bosses, and Boss minions and causes those enemies to regularly create a scattered few blueish-white orbs that hang in space, growing rapidly in size before detonating in short range Frost Novas.
	// These are damaging to any player, pet, or follower this hit and more dangerous still is their freezing effect, which leaves the frozen target helpless and motionless for a short duration.
	// Implementation: OnOwnerDied CreateThinker OnCreated DelayedAction Explosion+Damage

	"affix_frozen"
	{
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityTextureName"			"affix_frozen"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_POINT | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_AOE | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_IGNORE_BACKSWING"

		"AbilityCastRange"				"800"
		"AbilityCooldown"				"15"
		"AbilityDamage"					"100"

		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"explosion_delay"		"3"
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"explosion_radius"		"150"
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"stun_duration"		"3"
			}
		}

		"precache"
		{
			"particle"	"particles/warchasers/frozen/ancient_apparition_cold_feet.vpcf"
			"particle"	"particles/warchasers/frozen/ancient_apparition_ice_blast_explode.vpcf"
			"particle"	"particles/warchasers/frozen/tusk_ice_shards_projectile.vpcf"
			"particle"	"particles/warchasers/frozen/maiden_crystal_nova.vpcf"
		}

		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"CreateThinker"
	        {
	            "ModifierName"  "frozen_thinker"
	            "Target" 		"POINT"
	        }
		}

		"Modifiers"
		{
			"frozen_thinker"
			{
				"OnCreated"
				{
					// Attach the particles, also manages the explosion a bit after the explosion delay
					"RunScript"		
					{	
						"ScriptFile"	"abilities.lua"
						"Function"		"FrozenStart"
					}

					// We could do this in lua but I'm feeling elegant.
					"DelayedAction"
					{
						"Delay"		"%explosion_delay"
						"Action"
						{
							// Do the damage and apply modifier_frozen
							"ActOnTargets"
							{
							 	"Target"
							 	{
						            "Types"     "DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_BASIC | DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_HERO"
						            "Teams"     "DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_BOTH"
						            "Center"    "TARGET" //in this scope, this means the Thinker.
						            "Radius"    "%explosion_radius"
						        }
						        
						        "Action"
				         		{
						         	"Damage"
					         		{
					         			"Target"	"TARGET"
					         			"Type"		"DAMAGE_TYPE_MAGICAL"
					         			"Damage"	"%AbilityDamage"
					         		}
						         	
						         	"ApplyModifier"
						         	{
							 			"ModifierName"		"modifier_stunned"
							 			"Target"			"TARGET"
						         	}
						     	}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}

			"frozen_dummy_aura"
			{
				"Aura"					"frozen_aura_debuff"
				"Aura_Radius"			"%explosion_radius"
				"Aura_Teams"			"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_ENEMY"
				"Aura_Types"			"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_BASIC | DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_HERO"
				"Aura_Flags" 			"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_FLAG_INVULNERABLE"
				"Aura_ApplyToCaster"	"0"
			}

			//Slows a bit while in the radius
			"frozen_aura_debuff"
			{
				"IsHidden"	        "0"
				"IsDebuff"	        "1"
				"EffectName"		"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_cold_snap_status.vpcf"
				"EffectAttachType"	"follow_origin"
				"Properties"
				{
					"MODIFIER_PROPERTY_MOVESPEED_BONUS_CONSTANT" 	    "-25"
				}

			}

			"modifier_stunned"
			{
				"IsHidden"	        "0"
				"IsDebuff"	        "1"
				"Duration"	        "%stun_duration"
				"StatusEffectName"	"particles/status_fx/status_effect_frost_lich.vpcf"
				"StatusEffectPriority"	"15"
				"OverrideAnimation"	"ACT_DOTA_DISABLED"
				"States"
				{
					"MODIFIER_STATE_STUNNED"	"MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
					"MODIFIER_STATE_FROZEN"		"MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
				}
			}
			"frozen_ai"
	    	{
	    	"Passive"	"1"

	    	"ThinkInterval"		"1"
		    "OnIntervalThink"
		    	{
		    	"RunScript"
		    		{
		    		"ScriptFile"		"abilities.lua"
					"Function"			"frozen_ai"
		    		}
		    	}
	    	}
		}
